<span key="8820e7c54fc846708e6077bbfa58a154"><span offset-key="8820e7c54fc846708e6077bbfa58a154:0">Running JS Locally Concepts</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="5b64b753b330431f8ade86080bc60ab5"><span offset-key="5b64b753b330431f8ade86080bc60ab5:0">Match the commands </span>`ls`<span offset-key="5b64b753b330431f8ade86080bc60ab5:2">, </span>`cd`<span offset-key="5b64b753b330431f8ade86080bc60ab5:4">, </span>`pwd`<span offset-key="5b64b753b330431f8ade86080bc60ab5:6"> to their descriptions</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

        <span key="f83cb29fedee457989edfcff02b406ad">`ls`<span offset-key="f83cb29fedee457989edfcff02b406ad:1"> lists contents of current directory</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

        <span key="7d62a5d1cba04b418c2a27d976eec3fa">`cd`<span offset-key="7d62a5d1cba04b418c2a27d976eec3fa:1"> changes current directory</span></span>

        -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

            <span key="0662e282e66b4541bf5a01e447369251">`cd ..`<span offset-key="0662e282e66b4541bf5a01e447369251:1"> takes you up one level</span></span>

            <span key="b1ed3dafadea4cbfa7c506c8330a2887">`cd`<span offset-key="b1ed3dafadea4cbfa7c506c8330a2887:1"> alone takes you back home</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

        <span key="b1a31bd4f0ee4cf29f6b538dabb7a786">`pwd`<span offset-key="b1a31bd4f0ee4cf29f6b538dabb7a786:1"> returns current directory</span></span>

    <span key="68cfbb38cf924a2eb3a4b8c68e88b41b"><span offset-key="68cfbb38cf924a2eb3a4b8c68e88b41b:0">Label variables as either Primitive vs. Reference</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

        <span key="a120001d5659456ab22d96a2f1ed604b"><span offset-key="a120001d5659456ab22d96a2f1ed604b:0">primitives: strings, booleans, numbers, null and undefined</span></span>

        -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

            <span key="d0b92651df8f40b6ba77f95ca3301774"><span offset-key="d0b92651df8f40b6ba77f95ca3301774:0">primitives are immutable</span></span>

        <span key="e8ba8b38e29d4912b6c46cfbe50dcd3b"><span offset-key="e8ba8b38e29d4912b6c46cfbe50dcd3b:0">refereces: objects (including arrays)</span></span>

            <span key="c0e8a787b5f149c8ae9d78e481293567"><span offset-key="c0e8a787b5f149c8ae9d78e481293567:0">references are mutable</span></span>

    <span key="96e8f8d508a641239b83ea0678439aa8"><span offset-key="96e8f8d508a641239b83ea0678439aa8:0">Identify when to use </span>`.`<span offset-key="96e8f8d508a641239b83ea0678439aa8:2"> vs </span>`[]`<span offset-key="96e8f8d508a641239b83ea0678439aa8:4"> when accessing values of an object</span></span>

            <span key="fc7b79c654ab43b09186345af26834fa"><span offset-key="fc7b79c654ab43b09186345af26834fa:0">easier to read</span></span>

            <span key="d29dbf20b681406b8718b7b8bccede01"><span offset-key="d29dbf20b681406b8718b7b8bccede01:0">keys cannot begin with a number</span></span>

        <span key="2a79479ca9d7424197e5255f82ccec1f"><span offset-key="2a79479ca9d7424197e5255f82ccec1f:0">bracket notation </span>`object["key]`</span>

            <span key="6bf8c36c98dd4d9fb3c34f68db225b13"><span offset-key="6bf8c36c98dd4d9fb3c34f68db225b13:0">allows variables as keys</span></span>

        -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

            <span key="0a5bbe77c74d4518bef2d1f3b75d2ab7"><span offset-key="0a5bbe77c74d4518bef2d1f3b75d2ab7:0">strings that start with numbers can be use as keys</span></span>

        <span key="c54e153431f149a6b70692ad4124fe52"><span offset-key="c54e153431f149a6b70692ad4124fe52:0">array will be empty if there are no additional arguments</span></span>

    <span key="b47359c0930f4390a3ae8b5bbdff47c9"><span offset-key="b47359c0930f4390a3ae8b5bbdff47c9:0">Destructure an array to reference specific elements</span></span>

    <span key="2955ee3569a84d3593b34b912a132efc"><span offset-key="2955ee3569a84d3593b34b912a132efc:0">\`\`\`javascript</span></span>

    <span key="fe7ee172845046908ef1e3faecd22fbb"><span offset-key="fe7ee172845046908ef1e3faecd22fbb:0">let array = \[35,9\];</span></span>

    <span key="aad0731363a24dc19129790b321f7700"><span offset-key="aad0731363a24dc19129790b321f7700:0">let \[firstEl, secondEl\] = array;</span></span>

    <span key="4f7176b7fec04a94a32ecdda3ef635de"><span offset-key="4f7176b7fec04a94a32ecdda3ef635de:0">console.log(firstEl); // => 35</span></span>

    <span key="e80af7c6ef5b48499bd17a2a72a10ff7"><span offset-key="e80af7c6ef5b48499bd17a2a72a10ff7:0">console.log(secondEl); // => 9</span></span>

<span key="f38670fddda942b18b1c9220454e76cb"><span offset-key="f38670fddda942b18b1c9220454e76cb:0">// can also destructure using ... syntax let array = \[35,9,14\]; let \[head, ...tail\] = array; console.log(head); // => 35 console.log(tail); // => \[9, 14\]</span></span>

1

<span key="5f291e725428466aa5a16dcbabc37705"><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="5f291e725428466aa5a16dcbabc37705:0">-</span><span offset-key="5f291e725428466aa5a16dcbabc37705:1"> Destructure an object to reference specific values</span></span>

<span key="389442a12909479aba6e791ddb124b82"><span offset-key="389442a12909479aba6e791ddb124b82:0">Callbacks Lesson Concepts</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="9a0226f6cb0e4284b2700a3bfa0d6178"><span offset-key="9a0226f6cb0e4284b2700a3bfa0d6178:0">Given multiple plausible reasons, identify why functions are called "First Class Objects" in JavaScript.</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="19bfd0f438594c1a8fb5cd9d14854525"><span offset-key="19bfd0f438594c1a8fb5cd9d14854525:0">they can be stored in variables, passed as arguments to other functions, and serve as return value for a function</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="8a007cfe9f34453b94916067136b77ae"><span offset-key="8a007cfe9f34453b94916067136b77ae:0">supports same basic operations as other types (strings, bools, numbers)</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="04605f1fa91849b0a96f9c5f69ab84e1"><span offset-key="04605f1fa91849b0a96f9c5f69ab84e1:0">higher-order functions take functions as arguments or return functions as values</span></span>

    <span key="da201bd033514791804f7c88961cd566"><span offset-key="da201bd033514791804f7c88961cd566:0">Given a code snippet containing an anonymous callback, a named callback, and multiple </span>`console.log`<span offset-key="da201bd033514791804f7c88961cd566:2">s, predict what will be printed</span></span>

        <span key="bd3cb345153f43ecaff02303da38bd6f"><span offset-key="bd3cb345153f43ecaff02303da38bd6f:0">what is this referring to?</span></span>

    <span key="b186dd0340b4496fa5c42af730515177"><span offset-key="b186dd0340b4496fa5c42af730515177:0">Write a function that takes in a value and two callbacks. The function should return the result of the callback that is greater.</span></span>

    <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MDE1Nl8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

    Copied!

# 

<span key="4dd81511a35b418f93c91877a28c672d"><span offset-key="4dd81511a35b418f93c91877a28c672d:0">Scope Lesson Concepts</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="6fe6a4b58ee04595b15046ef6c914c72"><span offset-key="6fe6a4b58ee04595b15046ef6c914c72:0">Identify the difference between </span>`const`<span offset-key="6fe6a4b58ee04595b15046ef6c914c72:2">, </span>`let`<span offset-key="6fe6a4b58ee04595b15046ef6c914c72:4">, and </span>`var`<span offset-key="6fe6a4b58ee04595b15046ef6c914c72:6"> declarations</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="a0c24f4b15b341b3b6429767ad246d84">`const`<span offset-key="a0c24f4b15b341b3b6429767ad246d84:1"> - cannot reassign variable, scoped to block</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="50503b1d51be4045ae9bc7468e1c5f96">`let`<span offset-key="50503b1d51be4045ae9bc7468e1c5f96:1"> - can reassign variable, scoped to block</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="f9e3d453c929425fb1f68893c64cf332">`var`<span offset-key="f9e3d453c929425fb1f68893c64cf332:1"> - outdated, may or may not be reassigned, scoped to function. can be not just reassigned, but also redeclared!</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="b51c2c8b0bf34edd96f6a86131e4ebaf"><span offset-key="b51c2c8b0bf34edd96f6a86131e4ebaf:0">a variable will always evaluate to the value it contains regardless of how it was declared</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="d39894145c164e9f9d22a5cb7e5576bd"><span offset-key="d39894145c164e9f9d22a5cb7e5576bd:0">Explain the difference between </span>`const`<span offset-key="d39894145c164e9f9d22a5cb7e5576bd:2">, </span>`let`<span offset-key="d39894145c164e9f9d22a5cb7e5576bd:4">, and </span>`var`<span offset-key="d39894145c164e9f9d22a5cb7e5576bd:6"> declarations</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="5fd7d99252b842b29c1b6a77320a677f">`var`<span offset-key="5fd7d99252b842b29c1b6a77320a677f:1"> is function scopedâ€”so if you declare it anywhere in a function, the declaration (but not assignment) is "hoisted"</span></span>

        -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

            <span key="18d6d77578a447b4bacf7d1edb64fe3f"><span offset-key="18d6d77578a447b4bacf7d1edb64fe3f:0">so it will exist in memory as "undefined" which is bad and unpredictable</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="27fc1de104074956aa5a3436856a5f6b">`var`<span offset-key="27fc1de104074956aa5a3436856a5f6b:1"> will also allow you to redeclare a variable, while </span>`let`<span offset-key="27fc1de104074956aa5a3436856a5f6b:3"> or </span>`const`<span offset-key="27fc1de104074956aa5a3436856a5f6b:5"> will raise a syntax error. you shouldn't be able to do that!</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="f9cfe1e0d62e441280747babe596a8dd">`const`<span offset-key="f9cfe1e0d62e441280747babe596a8dd:1"> won't let you reassign a variable, but if it points to a mutable object, you will still be able to change the value by mutating the object</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="cf59a04689144f65954cc56a63aa84e0"><span offset-key="cf59a04689144f65954cc56a63aa84e0:0">block-scoped variables allow new variables with the same name in new scopes</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="c914aa4262bf4a99918711995d647faf"><span offset-key="c914aa4262bf4a99918711995d647faf:0">block-scoped still performs hoisting of all variables within the block, but it doesn't initialize to the value of </span>`undefined`<span offset-key="c914aa4262bf4a99918711995d647faf:2"> like </span>`var`<span offset-key="c914aa4262bf4a99918711995d647faf:4"> does, so it throws a specific reference error if you try to access the value before it has been declared</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="c815fc63840f44fab43a18b56f15c1b3"><span offset-key="c815fc63840f44fab43a18b56f15c1b3:0">if you do not use </span>`var`<span offset-key="c815fc63840f44fab43a18b56f15c1b3:2"> or </span>`let`<span offset-key="c815fc63840f44fab43a18b56f15c1b3:4"> or </span>`const`<span offset-key="c815fc63840f44fab43a18b56f15c1b3:6"> when initializing, it will be declared as globalâ€”THIS IS BAD</span></span>

        -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

            <span key="3e0b8b175209418a8364c2d10f3ef2df"><span offset-key="3e0b8b175209418a8364c2d10f3ef2df:0">if you assign a value without a declaration, it exists in the global scope (so then it would be accessible by all outer scopes, so bad). however, there's no hoisting, so it doesn't exist in the scope until after the line is run</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="a3c7751626984baa8f7a5fc84c6238cf"><span offset-key="a3c7751626984baa8f7a5fc84c6238cf:0">Predict the evaluation of code that utilizes function scope, block scope, lexical scope, and scope chaining</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="b4a48f5b885d4ce6b16533f3005fb842"><span offset-key="b4a48f5b885d4ce6b16533f3005fb842:0">scope of a program means the set of variables that are available for use within the program</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="e5b8dc7605a5422a89fda9a52b80d857"><span offset-key="e5b8dc7605a5422a89fda9a52b80d857:0">global scope is represented by the </span>`window`<span offset-key="e5b8dc7605a5422a89fda9a52b80d857:2"> object in the browser and the </span>`global`<span offset-key="e5b8dc7605a5422a89fda9a52b80d857:4"> object in Node.js</span></span>

        -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

            <span key="7bfff64e902f4f7cb001411a539a71dd"><span offset-key="7bfff64e902f4f7cb001411a539a71dd:0">global variables are available everywhere, and so increase the risk of name collisions</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="0f3a8db3d05742628cf19aab35fe7c33"><span offset-key="0f3a8db3d05742628cf19aab35fe7c33:0">local scope is the set of variables available for use within the function</span></span>

        -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

            <span key="9300488d70524c6a89ccf62aac2bc275"><span offset-key="9300488d70524c6a89ccf62aac2bc275:0">when we enter a function, we enter a new scope</span></span>

        -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

            <span key="fcc5a566959645c19ac3ed05ce7bf628"><span offset-key="fcc5a566959645c19ac3ed05ce7bf628:0">includes functions arguments, local variables declared inside function, and any variables that were already declared when the function is defined (hmm about that last one)</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="6e49ee2be69a422281c4c80ae41173e2"><span offset-key="6e49ee2be69a422281c4c80ae41173e2:0">for blocks (denoted by curly braces </span>`{}`<span offset-key="6e49ee2be69a422281c4c80ae41173e2:2">, as in conditionals or </span>`for`<span offset-key="6e49ee2be69a422281c4c80ae41173e2:4"> loops), variables can be block scoped</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="d3deda625d804e9cbf416b8313f462eb"><span offset-key="d3deda625d804e9cbf416b8313f462eb:0">inner scope does not have access to variables in the outer scope</span></span>

        -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

            <span key="30806f6e3b144b62b11f1268b5b58e39"><span offset-key="30806f6e3b144b62b11f1268b5b58e39:0">scope chainingâ€”if a given variable is not found in immediate scope, javascript will search all accessible outer scopes until variable is found</span></span>

        -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

            <span key="3a891ef3a1144c049fcc7541ac3dae54"><span offset-key="3a891ef3a1144c049fcc7541ac3dae54:0">so an inner scope can access outer scope variables</span></span>

        -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

            <span key="8eb5b192e94446eab545989ca415115a"><span offset-key="8eb5b192e94446eab545989ca415115a:0">but an outer scope can never access inner scope variables</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="5485ed77a49b449fac8504e922aec5ae"><span offset-key="5485ed77a49b449fac8504e922aec5ae:0">Define an arrow function</span></span>

    <span key="c815e98f472f49ea94809f5bf977c23b"><span offset-key="c815e98f472f49ea94809f5bf977c23b:0">\`\`\`javascript</span></span>

    <span key="43255ca12fea499095da1880c5f29fa6"><span offset-key="43255ca12fea499095da1880c5f29fa6:0">let arrowFunction = (param1, param2) => {</span></span>

    <span key="4d2c89f76a4d4c93a79a3bee7068b21f"><span offset-key="4d2c89f76a4d4c93a79a3bee7068b21f:0">let sum = param1 + param2;</span></span>

    <span key="89f782ea93fa40b8ab2db7ebea57819d"><span offset-key="89f782ea93fa40b8ab2db7ebea57819d:0">return sum;</span></span>

    <span key="229b82ace32c44aab9abcf9bb11b0f13"><span offset-key="229b82ace32c44aab9abcf9bb11b0f13:0">}</span></span>

<span key="8d88335ec4264baf96a27b9c51ee162c"><span offset-key="8d88335ec4264baf96a27b9c51ee162c:0">// with 1 param you can remove parens around parameters let arrowFunction = param => { param += 1; return param; }</span></span>

<span key="d74ecd97d7ff4ce8a3b6020abbae5c3d"><span offset-key="d74ecd97d7ff4ce8a3b6020abbae5c3d:0">// if your return statement is one line, you can use implied return let arrowFunction = param => param + 1;</span></span>

<span key="8977a6a869444127bf49d29e665e7703"><span offset-key="8977a6a869444127bf49d29e665e7703:0">// you don't have to assign to variable, can be anonymous // if you never need to use it again param => param + 1;</span></span>

<span key="ec64cd92c7dd46e791e03ec1e6d2c5d6"><span offset-key="ec64cd92c7dd46e791e03ec1e6d2c5d6:0">\`\`\`</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="a48e43d6eee2455b95a350f4b14f295b"><span offset-key="a48e43d6eee2455b95a350f4b14f295b:0">Given an arrow function, deduce the value of </span>`this`<span offset-key="a48e43d6eee2455b95a350f4b14f295b:2"> without executing the code</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="fc6dabe4a2f5404594ec565d8143f8a1"><span offset-key="fc6dabe4a2f5404594ec565d8143f8a1:0">arrow functions are automatically bound to the context they were declared in</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="f7096ab3f89b44c8a1393097297a79a6"><span offset-key="f7096ab3f89b44c8a1393097297a79a6:0">unlike regular function which use the context they are invoked in (unless they have been bound using </span>`Function#bind`<span offset-key="f7096ab3f89b44c8a1393097297a79a6:2">)</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="6d21cebffa1f4fd7993e3e25e1bfa6d4"><span offset-key="6d21cebffa1f4fd7993e3e25e1bfa6d4:0">if you implement an arrow function as a method in an object the context it will be bound to is NOT the object itself, but the global context</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="793e44bb40d84b92a8c58fffdd1fc41a"><span offset-key="793e44bb40d84b92a8c58fffdd1fc41a:0">so you can't use an arrow function to define a method directly</span></span>

        <span key="4c14bf8bd5fe4bbf81f3221f4ed67c37"><span offset-key="4c14bf8bd5fe4bbf81f3221f4ed67c37:0">\`\`\`javascript</span></span>

        <span key="c03016f1b4e74ed88578f1a988fa5e92"><span offset-key="c03016f1b4e74ed88578f1a988fa5e92:0">let obj = {</span></span>

        <span key="58ffd85de8c54a92af01ad552da618a2"><span offset-key="58ffd85de8c54a92af01ad552da618a2:0">name: "my object",</span></span>

        <span key="538f6089f3d84265962ddaef4294acbf"><span offset-key="538f6089f3d84265962ddaef4294acbf:0">unboundFunc: function () {</span></span>

        <span key="ea41f87541204a4ba10d0d3dd9b3e478"><span offset-key="ea41f87541204a4ba10d0d3dd9b3e478:0">return this.name;</span></span>

        <span key="2c1916fa48a744b49bb1af23b462efcb"><span offset-key="2c1916fa48a744b49bb1af23b462efcb:0">// this function will be able to be called on different objects</span></span>

        <span key="afd78f88ceec4961998903ddfcfba32f"><span offset-key="afd78f88ceec4961998903ddfcfba32f:0">},</span></span>

<span key="f0c94a1570084a768be74dcdd607adc4"><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="f0c94a1570084a768be74dcdd607adc4:0">// call unboundFunc on obj, we get "my object" console.log("unboundFunc: ", obj.unboundFunc()); // => "my object" // assign unboundFunc to a variable and call it let newFunc = obj.unboundFunc; // this newFunc will default to being called on global object console.log("newFunc: ",newFunc()); // => undefined // but you could bind it directly to a different object if you wanted console.log("newFunc: ", newFunc.bind(otherObj)()); // "my other object"</span></span>

35

<span key="4547b224a9d84bff90ca95e5dd36caa8"><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="4547b224a9d84bff90ca95e5dd36caa8:0">// meanwhile, obj.boundToGlobal will only ever be called on global object console.log("boundToGlobal: ", obj.boundToGlobal()); //=> undefined let newBoundFunc = obj.boundToGlobal; console.log("newBoundFunc: ", newBoundFunc()); // => undefined // even if you try to directly bind to another object, it won't work! console.log("newBoundFunc: ", newBoundFunc.bind(otherObj)()); // => undefined</span></span>

36

<span key="cf8f4b22a4c8490cbc36c1475ba6cf53"><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="cf8f4b22a4c8490cbc36c1475ba6cf53:0">// let's make a new function that will always be bound to the context // where we call our function maker let boundFunc = obj.makeFuncBoundToObj();// note that we're invoking, not just assigning console.log("boundFunc: ", boundFunc()); // => "my object" // we can't rebind this function console.log("boundFunc: ", boundFunc.bind(otherObj)()) // =>"my object"</span></span>

<span key="01d20153bb4c40048200d594af222a13"><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="01d20153bb4c40048200d594af222a13:0">// but if I call makeFuncBoundToObj on another context // the new bound function is stuck with that other context let boundToOther = obj.makeFuncBoundToObj.bind(otherObj)(); console.log("boundToOther: ", boundToOther()); // => "my other object" console.log("boundToOther: ", boundToOther.bind(obj)()) // "my other object"</span></span>

<span key="738beccad1c54628a99eee5ff5aa0f1e"><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="738beccad1c54628a99eee5ff5aa0f1e:0">// the return value of my immediately invoked function // shows that the context inside of the object is the // global object, not the object itself // context only changes inside a function that is called // on an object console.log("immediatelyInvokedFunc: ", obj.immediatelyInvokedFunc); // => undefined</span></span>

<span key="d5e21236701e4b1188808e55eea0201a"><span offset-key="d5e21236701e4b1188808e55eea0201a:0"> </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="d5e21236701e4b1188808e55eea0201a:1">-</span><span offset-key="d5e21236701e4b1188808e55eea0201a:2"> scope works like a dictionary that has all the variables that are available within a given block</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="d5e21236701e4b1188808e55eea0201a:3">,</span><span offset-key="d5e21236701e4b1188808e55eea0201a:4"> plus a pointer back the next offset-key="d5e21236701e4b1188808e55eea0201a:11">scopes</span><span offset-key="d5e21236701e4b1188808e55eea0201a:12"> until you reach the global scope</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="d5e21236701e4b1188808e55eea0201a:13">.</span><span offset-key="d5e21236701e4b1188808e55eea0201a:14"> so you can think about a whole given block's scope </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="d5e21236701e4b1188808e55eea0201a:15">as</span><span offset-key="d5e21236701e4b1188808e55eea0201a:16"> a kind </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="d5e21236701e4b1188808e55eea0201a:27">this</span><span offset-key="d5e21236701e4b1188808e55eea0201a:28"> is not to say that scope is actually implemented </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" <span key="d0bf07edeeaf482da80b4a883fab533a"><span offset-key="d0bf07edeeaf482da80b4a883fab533a:0"> </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="d0bf07edeeaf482da80b4a883fab533a:1">-</span><span offset-key="d0bf07edeeaf482da80b4a883fab533a:2"> context refers to the value </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="d0bf07edeeaf482da80b4a883fab533a:3">of</span><span offset-key="d0bf07edeeaf482da80b4a883fab533a:4"> the </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="d0bf07edeeaf482da80b4a883fab533a:5">\`</span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="d0bf07edeeaf482da80b4a883fab533a:6">this</span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="d0bf07edeeaf482da80b4a883fab533a:7">\`</span><span offset-key="d0bf07edeeaf482da80b4a883fab533a:8"> keyword</span></span>

        <span key="2823d7f53bfa4dd6990515faa2d47de5"><span offset-key="2823d7f53bfa4dd6990515faa2d47de5:0">you could also overwrite values or assign values to exist in a space where they should not exist</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="308dfcfa22084cfe9d5d1873260534c2"><span offset-key="308dfcfa22084cfe9d5d1873260534c2:0">if you call a function as a callback, it will set </span>`this`<span offset-key="308dfcfa22084cfe9d5d1873260534c2:2"> to be the outer function itself, even if the function you were calling is a method that was called on a particular object</span></span>

    <span key="69e9bd23e80640cfab79d675eca89a85"><span offset-key="69e9bd23e80640cfab79d675eca89a85:0">global.setTimeout(cat.purrMore, 5000); // 5 seconds later: TypeError: this.purr is not a function</span></span>

    Copied!

<span key="22eea97b341d42368d2ebaf94ff9fc5a"><span offset-key="22eea97b341d42368d2ebaf94ff9fc5a:0">we can use strict mode with </span>`"use strict";`<span offset-key="22eea97b341d42368d2ebaf94ff9fc5a:2"> this will prevent you from accessing the global object with </span>`this`<span offset-key="22eea97b341d42368d2ebaf94ff9fc5a:4"> in functions, so if you try to call </span>`this`<span offset-key="22eea97b341d42368d2ebaf94ff9fc5a:6"> in the global context and change a value, you will get a type error, and the things you try to access will be undefined</span></span>

<span key="37bee1946b0948039d5054a510d9ba1c"><span offset-key="37bee1946b0948039d5054a510d9ba1c:0">let sayMeow = cat.purrMore; console.log(sayMeow()); // TypeError: this.purr is not a function</span></span>

<span key="3f138c8ff30b409497c97705a9653d4d"><span offset-key="3f138c8ff30b409497c97705a9653d4d:0">// we can use the built in Function.bind to ensure our context, our </span>`this`<span offset-key="3f138c8ff30b409497c97705a9653d4d:2">, // is the cat object let boundCat = sayMeow.bind(cat);</span></span>

<span key="e67539f18da6489b8e8dc969eede64c8"><span offset-key="e67539f18da6489b8e8dc969eede64c8:0">boundCat(); // prints "meow"</span></span>

1

<span key="7eb4c9efc8ee4f8d8a6068731f6539a5"><span offset-key="7eb4c9efc8ee4f8d8a6068731f6539a5:0"> - \`bind\` can also work with arguments, so you can have a version of a function with particular arguments and a particular context. the first arg will be the context aka the \`this\` you want it to use. the next arguments will be the functions arguments that you are binding</span></span>

2

<span key="a6f1398146b7450181dc080362446c42"><span offset-key="a6f1398146b7450181dc080362446c42:0"> - if you just want to bind it to those arguments in particular, you can use \`null\` as the first argument, so the context won't be bound, just the arguments</span></span>

3

<span key="daabedf5f8cc4987ad4423c15d2cebda"><span offset-key="daabedf5f8cc4987ad4423c15d2cebda:0">- Given a code snippet, identify what \`this\` refers to</span></span>

4

<span key="fce576ac14164910bcbfb2546c2511b6"><span offset-key="fce576ac14164910bcbfb2546c2511b6:0"> - important to recognize the difference between scope and context</span></span>

5

<span key="bff9bf9fcc7d471dbf7408a09ca0ddda"><span offset-key="bff9bf9fcc7d471dbf7408a09ca0ddda:0"> - scope works like a dictionary that has all the variables that are available within a given block, plus a pointer back the next outer scope (which itself has pointers to new scopes until you reach the global scope. so you can think about a whole given block's scope as a kind of linked list of dictionaries) (also, this is not to say that scope is actually implemented in this way, that is just the schema that i can use to understand it)</span></span>

6

<span key="c96b901e71a3456a8b9a40652e8c1056"><span offset-key="c96b901e71a3456a8b9a40652e8c1056:0"> - context refers to the value of the \`this\` keyword</span></span>

7

<span key="60abacbabcc347cb9bd824cd8d96c017"><span offset-key="60abacbabcc347cb9bd824cd8d96c017:0"> - the keyword \`this\` exists in every function and it evaluates to the object that is currently invoking that function</span></span>

8

<span key="23f76bca55124880bea3c9f77895883e"><span offset-key="23f76bca55124880bea3c9f77895883e:0"> - so the context is fairly straightforward when we talk about methods being called on specific objects</span></span>

9

<span key="04cbe3b350444ade93d7c85517b52744"><span offset-key="04cbe3b350444ade93d7c85517b52744:0"> - you could, however, call an object's method on something other than that object, and then this would refer to the context where/how it was called, e.g.</span></span>

# 

<span key="d05f224f1b5c41ec9c554935c7cd57ad"><span offset-key="d05f224f1b5c41ec9c554935c7cd57ad:0">POJOs</span></span>

## 

<span key="3539347e7b4948f899a9698f3866d3fa"><span offset-key="3539347e7b4948f899a9698f3866d3fa:0">1. Label variables as either Primitive vs. Reference</span></span>

<span key="657967cc1c67496b9fe98635e23186f1"><span offset-key="657967cc1c67496b9fe98635e23186f1:0">Javascript considers most data types to be 'primitive', these data types are immutable, and are passed by value. The more complex data types: Array and Object are mutable, are considered 'reference' data types, and are passed by reference.</span></span>

    <span key="932b06f991724f38a1e0a0fd8f2be13b">`var`<span offset-key="932b06f991724f38a1e0a0fd8f2be13b:1"> is the historical keyword used for variable declaration.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="52900b852a6444ada62edf9c5325cd87">`var`<span offset-key="52900b852a6444ada62edf9c5325cd87:1"> declares variables in function scope, or global scope if not inside a function.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="d5f7782bbb784747bf274250855f53e4"><span offset-key="d5f7782bbb784747bf274250855f53e4:0">We consider </span>`var`<span offset-key="d5f7782bbb784747bf274250855f53e4:2"> to be </span>*deprecated*<span offset-key="d5f7782bbb784747bf274250855f53e4:4"> and it is never used in this course.</span></span>

    <span key="e212717ecba24db6b290aabea7ba253d">`let`<span offset-key="e212717ecba24db6b290aabea7ba253d:1"> is the keyword we use most often for variable declaration.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="ce7d1923b6c24977a66f1208a442bb9a">`let`<span offset-key="ce7d1923b6c24977a66f1208a442bb9a:1"> declares variables in block scope.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="b317d024ecf3497b84a514a5b2910a82"><span offset-key="b317d024ecf3497b84a514a5b2910a82:0">variables declared with </span>`let`<span offset-key="b317d024ecf3497b84a514a5b2910a82:2"> are re-assignable.</span></span>

    <span key="258675962f3d435c99b4c079cb5777fa">`const`<span offset-key="258675962f3d435c99b4c079cb5777fa:1"> is a specialized form of </span>`let`<span offset-key="258675962f3d435c99b4c079cb5777fa:3"> that can only be used to </span>**initialize**<span offset-key="258675962f3d435c99b4c079cb5777fa:5"> a variable.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="330b11baede04c2794a1e75446c4bdb3"><span offset-key="330b11baede04c2794a1e75446c4bdb3:0">Except when it is declared, you cannot assign to a </span>`const`<span offset-key="330b11baede04c2794a1e75446c4bdb3:2"> variable.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="cbb301c3a92648f2892d71c097b9b559">`const`<span offset-key="cbb301c3a92648f2892d71c097b9b559:1"> scopes variables the same way that </span>`let`<span offset-key="cbb301c3a92648f2892d71c097b9b559:3"> does.</span></span>

## 

<span key="dd7af936825041cc9fa34c8eeab2f9f3"><span offset-key="dd7af936825041cc9fa34c8eeab2f9f3:0">3. Predict the evaluation of code that utilizes function scope, block scope, lexical scope, and scope chaining</span></span>

<span key="3b565476c36a476a8832ba14790661ee"><span offset-key="3b565476c36a476a8832ba14790661ee:0">Consider this </span>`run`<span offset-key="3b565476c36a476a8832ba14790661ee:2"> function, inside which </span>`foo`<span offset-key="3b565476c36a476a8832ba14790661ee:4"> and </span>`bar`<span offset-key="3b565476c36a476a8832ba14790661ee:6"> have </span>`function scope`<span offset-key="3b565476c36a476a8832ba14790661ee:8">. </span>`i`<span offset-key="3b565476c36a476a8832ba14790661ee:10"> and </span>`baz`<span offset-key="3b565476c36a476a8832ba14790661ee:12"> are scoped to the block expression.</span></span>

##
